</header><div class="entry-content"><input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/><p><img alt="Two serving plates loaded with comforting vegan mashed potatoes topped with super hearty Lentil Mushroom Stew" class="aligncenter wp-image-31091 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-62.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes! 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>Friends, prepare yourselves for a hug in the form of a recipe.</p>
<p>Consider this your go-to dish when comfort food is on the brain. Not only is it hearty and satisfying, it’s also simple, requiring just <strong>10 basic ingredients</strong> and <strong>40 minutes</strong> to make (from start to finish). Let’s comfort food!</p>
<p><img alt="Metal serving tray filled with thyme, lentils, mushrooms, potatoes, shallots, and vegetable broth for making Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" class="aligncenter wp-image-31094 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes! BIG flavor, 10 ingredients, SUPER hearty #vegan #glutenfree #potatoes #lentils #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" height="2144" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-600x884.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-204x300.jpg 204w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-768x1131.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-695x1024.jpg 695w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-680x1001.jpg 680w" width="1456"/><span id="more-31080"></span></p>
<p>The base for this dish is a mushroom and lentil gravy/stew.</p>
<p>It starts with sautéed shallot and mushrooms seasoned with coconut aminos, salt, and pepper for rich, deep flavor. Then come lentils, thyme for aromatics, and vegetable broth. As that’s simmering away, start your mashed potatoes.</p>
<p><iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/JIsX8hkrrIE" width="680"></iframe></p>
<p><img alt="Pouring vegetable broth over lentils and veggies in a cast iron skillet to make gluten-free Lentil Mushroom Stew" class="aligncenter wp-image-31082 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes! BIG flavor, 10 ingredients, SUPER hearty #vegan #glutenfree #potatoes #lentils #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-39-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>The mashed potatoes are easy to make as well. Simply peel (or leave skin on for more texture), boil until tender, and mash!</p>
<p>You can go 100 different ways with seasoning mashed potatoes, but we kept things simple: a little salt, pepper, and olive oil, with a few dashes of almond milk for creaminess. SERIOUS yum. For more flavor, you could also add fresh garlic, herbs, or even some <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-vegan-parmesan-cheese/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">vegan parmesan cheese</a>.</p>
<p><img alt="Using a potato masher in a glass bowl of cooked potatoes to make vegan mashed potatoes" class="aligncenter wp-image-31084 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes! BIG flavor, 10 ingredients, SUPER hearty #vegan #glutenfree #potatoes #lentils #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-55-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>All that’s left to do is serve! For garnish, we went for more fresh thyme and a little parsley. Vegan parmesan adds a bit more flavor, but it’s certainly optional.</p>
<p><img alt="A hearty serving of fiber- and protein-packed Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" class="aligncenter wp-image-31087 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58.jpg" data-pin-description="DELICIOUS Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes! BIG flavor, 10 ingredients, SUPER hearty #vegan #glutenfree #potatoes #lentils #plantbased #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Lentil Mushroom Stew Over Mashed Potatoes" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/DELICIOUS-Lentil-Mushroom-Stew-over-Mashed-Potatoes-BIG-flavor-10-ingredients-SUPER-hearty-vegan-glutenfree-potatoes-lentils-plantbased-minimalistbaker-58-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>We hope you all LOVE this dish! It’s:</p>
<p>Super hearty<br/>
Comforting<br/>
Flavorful<br/>
Healthy<br/>
Fiber- + Protein-packed<br/>
Quick + Easy<br/>
&amp; So tasty</p>
<p>This would make a delicious easy weeknight meal for two or a hearty side for four. It’s reminiscent of <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-hour-vegan-shepherds-pie/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Shepherd’s Pie</a> but far easier to make! Plus, you can sauce up the filling a bit more so it’s more like mashed potatoes and gravy. Total swoon!</p>
<p>If you’re into hearty meals, check out our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/moroccan-lentil-stuffed-eggplant/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Moroccan Lentil Stuffed Eggplant</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/rich-red-curry-roasted-vegetables/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Rich Red Curry with Roasted Vegetables</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-pot-everyday-lentil-soup/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">1-Pot Everyday Lentil Soup</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/crispy-gluten-free-eggplant-parmesan/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Crispy Gluten-Free Eggplant Parmesan</a>, or <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/vegan-pumpkin-mac-n-cheese/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Vegan Pumpkin Mac ‘n’ Cheese</a>!</p>
<p>If you try this recipe, let us know! Leave a comment, rate it, and don’t forget to tag a photo <a href="https://www.instagram.com/minimalistbaker/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">#minimalistbaker</a> on Instagram. Cheers, friends!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Lentil Mushroom Stew over Mashed Potatoes</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
		Crazy delicious and hearty mushroom lentil stew gravy over mashed potatoes! Entirely vegan, gluten-free, and grain-free. A delicious and easy-to-make 10-ingredient meal or side!	</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-times-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-name">Prep Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time wprm-recipe-prep_time-minutes">10</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time-unit wprm-recipe-prep_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-name">Cook Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time wprm-recipe-cook_time-minutes">30</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-cook_time-unit wprm-recipe-cook_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-total-time-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-total-time-name">Total Time</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time wprm-recipe-total_time-minutes">40</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-total_time-unit wprm-recipe-total_timeunit-minutes">minutes</span> </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-servings-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-servings-name">Servings:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-servings">4</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-servings-unit"></span>
</div>

					Entree				</span>

					Gluten-Free, Grain-Free, Vegan				</span>

<span class="wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-freezer-friendly-name">Freezer Friendly</span>

					1 month				</span>

<span class="wprm-recipe-does-it-keep">
					4 Days				</span>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="34142" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> - <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="34142" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">POTATOES</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">pound</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">yellow potatoes, peeled and quartered evenly (I left on some skin for texture)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Sea salt + black pepper to taste</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1-2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">olive oil (if avoiding oil, add more almond milk or vegetable broth)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2-4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">unsweetened almond milk or vegetable broth (for added moisture)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">MUSHROOM LENTIL GRAVY</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">water</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or avocado or olive oil)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chopped shallot</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sliced cremini (or button) mushrooms</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1-2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Coconut-Secret-Raw-Aminos-Pack/dp/B00CMYMRL2/?tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">coconut aminos</a></span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Pinch</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">each salt and pepper</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chopped fresh thyme </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub rosemary // use dried if fresh is unavailable)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2/3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">dry green lentils</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(rinsed + drained // <em>optional</em>: soak overnight in cool water to improve digestibility)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2-3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-1-pot-vegetable-broth/" target="_blank">vegetable broth</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or store-bought)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">tomato paste</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<em>optional</em>)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/" target="_blank">mashed potatoes </a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(recipe above // for thickness)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">GARNISH optional</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Fresh chopped parsley</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-vegan-parmesan-cheese/" target="_blank">Vegan Parmesan Cheese</a></span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Heat a large rimmed pan over medium heat. Once hot, add oil or water and shallot and sauté for 2 minutes, stirring occasionally.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Add mushrooms and coconut aminos and increase heat to medium-high. Sauté for 5 minutes, stirring frequently. Add a pinch of salt and pepper.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add thyme, lentils, and 2 cups (480 ml // or the smaller end of the range if adjusting recipe size) vegetable broth. Bring to a low boil over medium-high heat. Once boiling, reduce heat to a simmer and cook on low for about 20 minutes, adding more broth as needed if the mixture looks dry.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">In the meantime, add potatoes to a large pot and cover with water so they are just submerged. Bring to a boil on high heat and cook for 12-15 minutes or until they slide off easily when pierced with a knife.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Once tender, drain potatoes and add back to pot or a mixing bowl. Season with salt, pepper, and a bit of olive oil and mash until tender and fluffy. For added moisture in place of oil, add unsweetened plain almond milk or vegetable broth.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Once lentils are tender, taste sauce and adjust flavor as needed, adding more salt or coconut aminos for saltiness, pepper for spice, or tomato paste for more depth of flavor (optional - we didn't find it necessary). Turn off heat and let the mixture rest so flavors can deepen. Add the 2 Tbsp (30 g // or more as needed) mashed potatoes to the lentil mushroom stew and stir in to thicken.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">To serve, divide mashed potatoes between serving plates or bowls and top with desired amount of lentil and mushroom gravy. Garnish with fresh parsley, vegan parmesan cheese, or more thyme, if desired.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Store leftovers separately, covered, up to 4 days in the refrigerator or in the freezer up to 1 month. Reheat on the stovetop or in a 350 degree F (176 C) oven until hot.</div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>

<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Heather Johnston" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/26379f460323d9bd2caedab747fc021e?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/26379f460323d9bd2caedab747fc021e?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Heather Johnston" width="96"><span itemprop="name">Heather Johnston</span> <span class="says">says</span> </img></p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-863919">February 16, 2020 at 9:00 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I have been adapting to a whole food plant based way of eating and this has become a “go-to” recipe for lentils that I seem to be making on a weekly basis now.  There is something that is so satisfying as lentil gravy on mash potatoes.   I have been using shiitake mushrooms with it and for the mash potatoes I don’t bother peeling for extra nutrition and it makes it even less work!  Easy recipe.   This is so yummy.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>I had some leftover lentils I needed to use up.  This recipe is absolutely fantastic.  So comforting, savory, and satisfying.  My somewhat picky teen boy even liked it.  Anything with mashed potatoes is usually a win- this did not disappoint!  I didn’t use the optional tomato paste (I didn’t want to then have tomato paste to have to use up), skipped the oil also.  Otherwise I made it pretty much as is.  I don’t eat a lot of  lentils- this will certainly change that!  This will be in regular rotation.  Thanks for all the great recipes.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-839700">
<article id="article-comment-839700">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Lily" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9ac7869ff0f6c30051f76de5e0cd0bc5?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9ac7869ff0f6c30051f76de5e0cd0bc5?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Lily" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Lily</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-839700">November 4, 2019 at 7:32 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I have made this a couple of times. </p>
<p>Tonight, I made it with mushroom stock (store bought, College Inn brand) and it really brought a delicious depth of flavor. I also used soy sauce instead of coconut aminos. The first time I made this, I used dried thyme and this time I used fresh – the fresh was 100x better and didn’t leave chewy pieces the way the dried thyme did. </p>
<p>However, my lentils were not evenly cooking with the 2 c of broth (the ones on top stayed hard because 2 c did not cover them completely), so I ended up adding more and more liquid, using 4 c total (I used the whole container of broth) and had to cover my pan as well. I think my lentils did not cook evenly the first time either, but it’s an easy enough fix that I wouldn’t dock the instructions (it could totally be something I’m doing wrong). This is a great recipe regardless! I served it with your Best Damn Vegan Mashed Potatoes recipe and used fresh roasted garlic in the potatoes.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-837668">
<article id="article-comment-837668">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Lena" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fef397a00d560d340667b69bb51db5db?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fef397a00d560d340667b69bb51db5db?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Lena" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Lena</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-837668">October 25, 2019 at 7:16 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Tasty, versatile dish! I soaked a package of dried porcini mushrooms and added them along with the button mushrooms, and threw in some of the soaking water as well since I was a little short on broth. I accidentally used dried oregano instead of dried thyme (whoops!) but it still turned out good. I added a splash of red wine vinegar at the end for a little extra zip and served it over egg noodles.</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<p>This dish is so much more than the sum of its parts–and that’s considering how awesome its individual parts are. I doubled the recipe, using tamari instead of coconut aminos and vegetable broth to mash the potatoes. I mostly eyeballed amounts, and the final product is still scrumptious. As promised, this recipe was definitely easy and quick to make.</p>
<p>I’ve been writing this review for a while now because I keep stopping to eat more. True story.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Very yummy and comforting! This recipe goes into our family favourites! Kids and grownups loved it!</p>
<p>I’ve made this recipe twice and first time lentils were not nearly tender after 20 minutes, it took about 40-50 minutes for them to cook through. I used brown unsoaked lentils. Second time I pre-cooked lentils in Pressure cooker for 7 minutes and it turned out amazing.</p>

<p>Deeeeeeellllliiiiiiicccciiiioooouuuusss !!!<br/>
I’m a bit cheeky and added some white wine to the lentils, but I’ve made them before and they’re really good with or without white wine ;) Also, I used veggie cube broth and even with this cheep/lazy alternative the meal was amazing! And the mashed potatoes were just as good as they would be with milk &amp; butter if not better! I never thought to use veggie broth instead of milk!<br/>
Thanks for another great recipe!</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-807896">June 8, 2019 at 3:54 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I have tried this recipe 4 times and each time the lentils take close to an hour to cook. I am using red lentils, I am almost using to much liquid so I know they are not in want of that, I’ve trie this on low, medium low and high heat but nothing gets the time to 20 minutes. what am I doing wrong? do the lentils need to be soaked? I’ve looked for other red lentil recipes and they all say 20 minutes as well but nothing about soaking.</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to andrew" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-807896" data-commentid="807896" data-postid="31080" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-807896" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>

<ul class="children">
<li class="comment byuser comment-author-dana bypostauthor even depth-2" id="comment-808085">
<article id="article-comment-808085">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Dana @ Minimalist Baker</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-808085">June 10, 2019 at 12:43 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Andrew, red lentils should generally take only 5-10 minutes to cook – they’re so small and tender. Green and brown and black varieties can take longer. One option is to cook the lentils separate in boiling water until tender to speed cooking, and then add them to the sauce. Hope that helps!</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to Dana @ Minimalist Baker" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-808085" data-commentid="808085" data-postid="31080" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-808085" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>

<li class="comment odd alt depth-2" id="comment-836754">
<article id="article-comment-836754">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for OkraW" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/15e2dbf2a2c0198d02d806a926c49f14?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/15e2dbf2a2c0198d02d806a926c49f14?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for OkraW" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">OkraW</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-836754">October 21, 2019 at 11:57 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Andrew, are you maybe using whole red lentils? There is a split version that does not need to be soaked (although I always soak at least for 30 mins with split lentils). For whole lentils, I’d still soak overnight or least 8 hours. It should quicken the cook time significantly once you get cooking!</p>
</div>

<p>I haven’t made this yet, though looking at it and reading the comments I can’t wait to fix this  for my daughter. That being said, she is the only non meat eater in our family. Fixing larger meals for her is a waste because most recipes are made to feed a family not an individual.</p>
<p>My question is besides the mashed potatoes, could this recipe be freezer friendly?</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-790181">
<article id="article-comment-790181">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for meeshy-keen" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/8ee52b2d4a23292706e23477ce1192a0?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/8ee52b2d4a23292706e23477ce1192a0?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for meeshy-keen" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">meeshy-keen</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-790181">March 19, 2019 at 8:17 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This stew was SO SO delicious and hearty. My lentils took a bit longer to cook (about 10 minutes more), so I just kept them simmering, adding hot water little by little if they looked dry, until the lentils were perfect. I served these with the aptly named “Best Damn Vegan Mashed Potatoes” instead of the mash in this recipe. The chives and garlic in the potatoes went really well with the stew. Served at a dinner party and multiple people asked me to send them the recipe. :)</p>

<p>Finally tried this today after saving to pinterest ages ago. It was absolutely fantastic! I was making it ahead of time, so wasn’t making the mashed potatoes, so instead of mashed potatoes to thicken, I used 2 tablespoons cornstarch beaten with 1/4 cup of water. Worked great. Can’t wait to make again – it was such a warm and hearty dish to eat a cold winter’s evening.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-783887">
<article id="article-comment-783887">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Barbara" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/abfbe51589eca0e8468334a9357bc59b?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/abfbe51589eca0e8468334a9357bc59b?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Barbara" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Barbara</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-783887">January 26, 2019 at 6:57 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This is pure comfort food to be sure.<br/>
I used black lentils that I soaked all day. I added carrots to mine too. I also used my InstaPot to cook the stew. Decreased liquid to 2 cups and cooked the stew for 15 minutes on high.<br/>
The flavors were perfectly blended. I let the stew bubble on the sauté setting for five additional minutes to further reduce liquids befor stirring in mashed potatoes.<br/>
I used a combination of red and gold baby potatoes for the mash. I added vegan keifer I made in the InstaPot to give the potatoes a tangy flavor.  Yum!<br/>
This recipe is husband approved.  And will definitely make it again and serve over polenta.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Judy! We recommend using uncooked lentils (or soaked) and adding them along with thyme and vegetable broth for best results in the recipe! If you try out the recipe using cooked lentils, report back on how it goes!</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Jillian Pius" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1e6ebf755fee597e127f1559e0567162?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1e6ebf755fee597e127f1559e0567162?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Jillian Pius" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Jillian Pius</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-777462">December 10, 2018 at 8:23 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made the mashed potatoes the night before in my instant pot.<br/>
I used the same amount of potatoes and put just enough water to cover them in the instant pot, then cook on high heat/pressure for 10 minutes. Instead of using vegetable broth in the potatoes,  I used the leftover potato-water. </p>
<p>It was really yummy!</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Gabi" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a004ccc5a823875c512e32207f73c886?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a004ccc5a823875c512e32207f73c886?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Gabi" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Gabi</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-776756">December 3, 2018 at 3:16 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I have been making recipes off this amazing site for awhile now, and this recipe was so delicious that I decided I just have to leave a review and start contributing.  I only used 2 cups vegetable broth but next time I will use more because it would be nice to have more sauciness to put over the potatoes. I also sauteed a bunch of garlic in 2 Tbsp of avocado oil and then added that into the mashing of potatoes for some extra flavor. Did not end up using tomato paste. Must try! I will definitely be making this again</p>

I see someone else blended a little of the gravy and I love that idea!</p>

<p>Thanks for this yummy recipe – just made for the 1st time tonight! My ‘meat-loving’ hubby even liked it.  I sub’d in Tamari Sauce for Coconut Aminos (didn’t have).  I did use the tomato paste, plus added a generous splash of red wine.  Very happy I doubled the recipe – leftovers!</p>

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for senora grayson" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7e726a8a9bf0837020136f183b0def1?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7e726a8a9bf0837020136f183b0def1?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for senora grayson" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">senora grayson</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-768756">October 11, 2018 at 6:18 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made it and it was delicious! I work for a health care facility where I cook for home bound people with HIV and various cancers. I make a bunch of meals during the week and freeze them to be delivered every Tuesday. I wanted to start making one vegetarian or vegan meal a month to see how the clients like it so I started with this! A couple of  changes- I added more veggies to the stew, spinach carrot and zucchini (because I had it on hand). Then I swapped out the yellow potatoes for sweet potatoes and cauliflower. I added brown butter, a little cayenne and minced garlic. Wish I could show you the pics, it turned out great! Thanks a lot!</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-768266">October 7, 2018 at 5:24 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made this recipe and it was so hearty and delicious. I put my cooked potatoes in the food processor and whipped them up and that was SO delicious with it. I added garlic powder and rosemary because I love that. My roommate who doesn’t like the texture of mushrooms loved it but had to eat around the mushrooms so when she made the recipe herself, she bought Pacifica brand mushroom soup and used that instead because she doesn’t like the texture. I know many people don’t love the texture of mushrooms so if it looks good to you, try that! This is one of my favorite recipes I’ve tried so far.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-761783">
<article id="article-comment-761783">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Lizzie" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/680342fb4723745e6f26b700c89b4f51?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/680342fb4723745e6f26b700c89b4f51?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Lizzie" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Lizzie</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-761783">August 14, 2018 at 10:39 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>First of all, this was delicious!! The recipe is easy to follow and I’d highly recommend! Something about the combo of mashed potatoes and lentils was just absolutely heavenly. My ONLY critique/suggestion is regarding the cook time for the lentils. As others point out, 20 min on low is definitely not long enough. I didn’t time how long it took to cook after my 20 min timer went off, but very possibly was closer to 40 min. I waited until most of the liquid had dissolved from the 2cups of veg broth &amp; it was perfect. The video was extremely helpful in showing the type of consistency that the strew should have after fully cooked.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-756079">June 18, 2018 at 12:28 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was so flavorful and lovely. I’ll admit I was skeptical before making it, thinking there was no way such simple ingredients could come together into a comforting dish (and help me get over my craving for mashed potatoes, steak and gravy). And I was reeeeaaaally hesitating with those 2 tablespoons of thyme – it just seemed like an awful lot. But I trusted the recipe and went forward. </p>
<p>Boy am I glad I did! I’m so surprised by how comforting and delicious this is! I made it for my meal prep, can’t wait to eat it all this week!<br/>
I made it with cauliflower mash, which made it even healthier, but kept it satisfying. Thanks Dana, you’ve done it again!</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-even depth-1" id="comment-753571">
<article id="article-comment-753571">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Chris W" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a1d1ab404c3859ea802799884e590bb3?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a1d1ab404c3859ea802799884e590bb3?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Chris W" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Chris W</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-753571">May 23, 2018 at 7:26 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made this last night for dinner, and it was excellent. I didn’t have tomato paste, so I substituted red miso with a splash of apple cider vinegar, and it seemed to work just fine! </p>
<p>I used rosemary instead of thyme, and rather than add the chopped herbs to the stew, I bruised a sprig of rosemary and added it to the pan, removing it after about 15 minutes. Rosemary can be overpowering for me, and this gave it a great flavor without being overwhelming.</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Nico" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c498d331f9dbbc8a87ff394d4bb2956d?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c498d331f9dbbc8a87ff394d4bb2956d?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Nico" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Nico</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-752832">May 16, 2018 at 12:26 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This is one of my favorite things I’ve cooked – I made some tweaks as I have no dietary restrictions and used what was on hand (butter and half &amp; half in the potatoes, chicken broth instead of veggie broth, soy sauce instead of coconut aminos, included the tomato paste) – but I’m certain the dish would be good without my changes. I found the fresh thyme to be a key player in the flavor, so include it if you can! I served the dish in bowls topped some garlicky sautéed kale. It all held up wonderfully as leftovers as well.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-752639">
<article id="article-comment-752639">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Leslie Ewing" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/98b0c7c8a429427a304a0e6f738c480f?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/98b0c7c8a429427a304a0e6f738c480f?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Leslie Ewing" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Leslie Ewing</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-752639">May 14, 2018 at 7:10 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I have made this 3 times now. My husband and I are on the Whole Foods Plant Based Diet right now, so the first time I made this, I mashed the potatoes (and skins) with vegetable broth,  and water sautéed the onions and mushrooms. Yum, yum, yum.</p>
<p>The second time I made this, I forgot to get fresh thyme so I used dried thyme. So good. Also, I put it on top of baked potatoes.  Less muss, less fuss, still good.</p>
<p>The last time I made the Lentil Mushroom Stew I put it on spelt macaroni. My husband says that was his favorite way of eating it.</p>
<p>By the way, I did not need to add the potato to thicken it. I am amazed at how simple, yet how yummy it is! Thanks!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was so good! I am having a ‘minimalist baker week’ – this is the fourth recipe of yours I made this week! We are not vegan so I made regular mashed potatoes since so far I have not yeat eaten vegan mashed potatoes that I enjoyed as much. I also used about double the amount of mushrooms because we just really love them. At the end we each added a teaspoon of nutritional yeast to our plates. The whole family enjoyed it, my 1-year-old ate almost an adult sized portion and my 3-year-old kept asking for more even after she’d had dessert!</p>

<p>Hey Dana!<br/>
I made this for a Shabbat meal and my entire (carnivore) family loved it! I subbed the potato mash with cauliflower mash (fewer calories and more deliciousness ) and added dried chili flakes and fresh lemon juice for more flavor.  Adding some of the mash to the stew for thickness was such a good tip!<br/>
Your recipes are an amazing tool to show my family and friends how delicious and easy it is to be vegan, thank you so much for all the fabulous content you’re putting out :)</p>

<li class="comment byuser comment-author-support even depth-2" id="comment-751389">
<article id="article-comment-751389">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Support @ Minimalist Baker" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9501d522e8b6b56b741d5c9b17c76182?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9501d522e8b6b56b741d5c9b17c76182?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Support @ Minimalist Baker" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Support @ Minimalist Baker</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-751389">May 2, 2018 at 6:38 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Emma! You can easily sub gluten-free tamari or soy sauce! Coconut aminos is a soy-free alternative to soy sauce, with a less pungent flavor. I usually double the amount of coconut aminos I would add to a recipe that calls for soy sauce. So, if a recipe calls for 2 Tbsp soy sauce/tamari, I’d probably add 3-4 Tbsp coconut aminos. Hope that helps!</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to Support @ Minimalist Baker" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-751389" data-commentid="751389" data-postid="31080" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-751389" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-750573">
<article id="article-comment-750573">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Jes" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/071d9e7942477bf77f3ece4ac08b4080?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/071d9e7942477bf77f3ece4ac08b4080?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Jes" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Jes</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-750573">April 24, 2018 at 2:32 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Gorgeous! This is a lovely recipe. It’s autumn/fall here in Australia, so this is perfect for the cooler weather.  I’ll add some spinach or kale next time, just to sneak more greens in. I think it’ll work nicely with the flavours of the broth. I worked with what I had, so some minor changes:</p>
<p>– Canned lentils, instead of dried.<br/>
– 1tbsp tamari, instead of coconut aminio<br/>
– 1 cube of massel stock with 1 cup of hot water, instead of x2 cups of broth.<br/>
– Chives, instead of shallots<br/>
– Added some garlic</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-749582">April 14, 2018 at 3:49 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Absolutely delicious! I will definitely make this again. Maybe we’re just big eaters, but I shared this with one other person and we finished it all, so I might double it next time to have leftovers or if I’m serving three or four people. I made the recipe as written, except using soy sauce instead of aminos and dried rosemary instead of fresh. I soaked the lentils and had no problem digesting them. Thanks for another absolute winner of a recipe Dana!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Just had this for dinner and it was so delicious!  I had to add extra water as the lentils were simmering, but other than that, I followed the recipe exactly. I happened to have an open can of tomato paste, so I added that and the addition was lovely. Love the idea of adding mashed potatoes to thicken the gravy! Will definitely be making this again!</p>

<li class="comment even thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-749088">
<article id="article-comment-749088">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Shannon" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/28a32fe7feeaae6542ffe7192f7bd7a1?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/28a32fe7feeaae6542ffe7192f7bd7a1?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Shannon" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Shannon</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-749088">April 8, 2018 at 6:42 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I used water to Sauté, subbed better than bouillon for broth and yellow onion for shallot, left out the tomato paste and salt, and used an Italian dry spice mix instead of the herbs mentioned. I did have to add quite a bit more water than was called for but that may have been because the stove I was cooking on doesn’t have low enough heat to simmer. I didn’t miss the oil or tomato paste at all. It was a huge hit! I will definitely be making it again.</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-748907">
<article id="article-comment-748907">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Manuela" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/084abe9f3ffaa9f6e26bde897af1e996?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/084abe9f3ffaa9f6e26bde897af1e996?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Manuela" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Manuela</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-748907">April 6, 2018 at 6:48 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>In the wise words of Owen Wilson; “Wow.”</p>
<p>Didn’t think your recipes could get any better, but here we are. This was perfect timing too, as I had some mushrooms I wanted to use up. </p>
<p>My lentils and mushrooms didn’t turn out as stew-y as yours did, despite using 3 cups of broth in addition to more water, but I think that could have been because my stove is finicky and difficult to get mid-range temperatures (it’s either blazing hot or lighter than a simmer), so my temp could have been too high. I think next time I’ll add even more mushrooms. </p>
<p>Other than that, flavors were spot on. Major comfort dish here; seriously recommend.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-748674">April 4, 2018 at 11:15 am</a></time></p> </header>

<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to Lisa Lorraine Machat" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-748674" data-commentid="748674" data-postid="31080" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-748674" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>

<ul class="children">
<li class="comment byuser comment-author-dana bypostauthor even depth-2" id="comment-748676">
<article id="article-comment-748676">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Dana @ Minimalist Baker</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/lentil-mushroom-stew-over-mashed-potatoes/?t=1582403911#comment-748676">April 4, 2018 at 11:22 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>You can easily sub gluten-free tamari or soy sauce! Coconut aminos is a soy-free alternative to soy sauce, with a less pungent flavor. I usually double the amount of coconut aminos I would add to a recipe that calls for soy sauce. So, if a recipe calls for 2 Tbsp soy sauce/tamari, I’d probably add 3-4 Tbsp coconut aminos. Hope that helps!</p>
</div>

				jQuery(document).ready(function () {

					function mgclInit() {
						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.no-lightbox').click(mgclOnClick);

						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('a.set-target').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('a.set-target').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.set-target').click(mgclOnClick);
					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
